---
layout: paradigm
paradigm: ADJ_REHTI
---
### ` ADJ_REHTI `

* _ti stems, ti : de variations_
* Universal POS is ADJ and legacy POS is ADJECTIVE
* suffixes use front vowel harmony
* KOTUS paradigm used in their dictionary is 5-F
* The lemmas must end in * ti * (which will be deleted to form an invariant stub) and the regex matching the lemma is ` [ÄÖYIEĒÉÍäöyieíüýéőèěęøæõ][^aou]*ti `
